### Round 2: Brazilian Grand Prix
*Date: 1975-01-26*

### Round 5: Monaco Grand Prix
*Date: 1975-05-11*

#### Qualifying Results

### Round 8: Dutch Grand Prix
*Date: 1975-06-22*
